\n15: #### `HeadSeriesRef`\n16: \n17: `HeadSeriesRef` is simply a 64bit counter that increments when a new series comes in.\n18: Due to series churn, the set of actively used `HeadSeriesRef`s may be well above zero (e.g. 0-10M may not be used, and 10M-11M is active)\n19: \n20: ","endLine":20,"startLine":14},{"content":"25: Notes:\n26: 1) M-mapped Head chunks, while they use `HeadSeriesRef`s,
